<a id="s14-3"></a>

## 14.3. Bestiary

This is a comprehensive list of every single enemy in Phantasy Star IV, including bosses, given in alphabetical order for ease of reference.

The layout of each enemy description is as follows:

<!-- MIXED -->

<!-- MODERNIZE:unknown -->

```
¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯  |          ||           ||          |
 E n e m y   N a m e                  |       HP ||       EXP ||      MST |
_____________________________________ |__________||___________||__________|
¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|   __________    Item enemy may drop
   | Enemy Type                    |  / Location \
   |                               | |            ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
   | Encounter: Type of Battle     |(| Where the enemy is encountered
   |                               | |
   | Number Encountered:     Range |(| ____________
   |_______________________________| |/ Techniques \
   |Fir|Wtr|Nrg|Frc|Grv|Elc|Rad|Lgt|(|              ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
   |   |>+<|   | - | + |   |   | x | | The enemy's Techniques
   |¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|¯¯¯¯¯¯¯|(| ________
   | Death |Destroy|Cleanse|  EMP  | |/ Skills \
   |   x   |   /   |   /   |   x   |(|          ¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
   |¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯| | The enemy's Skills
   | Paralysis, Sleep & Seals? Yes |(|
   |_______________________________| |_____________________________________
   |¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯¯
   | NOTES: Any additional information about the enemy
   |_______________________________________________________________________
```

The section between Number Encountered and the Notes gives details of the enemy's weaknesses and resistances. The first row of eight boxes represents the eight elements in the game, in the following order:

Fire Water Energy Force Gravity Electric Radiation Light Fir Wtr Nrg Frc Grv Elc Rad Lgt

Any symbols underneath each element correspond to a certain affinity, as follows (no symbol indicates the enemy receives normal damage):

x Immunity - the enemy takes 1 HP damage from this element

- Resistance - the enemy takes reduced damage from this element

+ Weakness - the enemy takes increased damage from this element >+< - extreme weakness - may take as much as double damage

XXX Unknown - this element cannot be used at the time

The rows beneath the elements indicate the enemy's susceptibility to the various death and status effects. A tick (/) means that the enemy can be affected, and a cross (x) shows that it is immune. A 'Yes' or 'No' in the bottom box says if the enemy can be affected by Paralysis, Sleep and Seals.

In the above example, the enemy is weak against water and gravity (very weak against water), resistant to force and immune from light. It can be affected by destroy and cleanse abilities, but not death or EMP ones, and can be paralysed or put to sleep.

To find an enemy more quickly, press CTRL+F and type 'BST' followed by the initial letter of the enemy. For example, to find Dominator type 'BSTD' and press enter. This will take you to the first entry with that letter.

<!-- MIXED -->
